3. Now, we check if 4387 is divisible by 5. If the last digit of a number is either 0 or 5, then the number is divisible by 5. The last digit of 4387 is 7, which is not equal to 0 or 5. Therefore, 4387 is not divisible by 5.

4. Next, we check if 4387 is divisible by 7. One way to do this is to subtract two times the last digit from the rest of the number (except the last digit). If the result is divisible by 7, then the original number is also divisible by 7. So we have: 438 - 2 × 7 = 424. Since 424 is not divisible by 7, 4387 is not divisible by 7.

5. Finally, we can check if 4387 is divisible by 11. Similar to the test for 7, we subtract two times the last digit (7) from the rest of the number (438). The result is 438 - 2 × 7 = 424. Since 424 is not divisible by 11, 4387 is not divisible by 11.

Since we have checked all prime numbers up to the square root of 4387, and none of them divide 4387, we can conclude that 4387 is a prime number.

Therefore, 4387 is a prime number.

2. Next, check divisibility of 7631 by prime numbers up to the square root of 7631.

   a. Check divisibility by 2: 7631 is not divisible by 2 since it is an odd number.

   b. Check divisibility by 3: Sum the digits of 7631 (7+6+3+1 = 17). 17 is not divisible by 3, so 7631 is not divisible by 3.

   c. Check divisibility by 5: Since the last digit of 7631 is not 0 or 5, it is not divisible by 5.

   d. Check divisibility by 7: Apply the divisibility rule for 7 (subtract twice the last digit from the truncated number): 763 - (2 * 1) = 761. Since 761 is not divisible by 7, neither is 7631.

   e. Continue by checking divisibility by 11, 13, 17, and so on until you reach the square root of 7631. However, since the previous tests have not found any divisors, it is enough to conclude that 7631 is a prime number.

Therefore, 7631 is a prime number.

Let's begin checking divisibility by prime numbers:

3. Check divisibility by 2: 5513 is not divisible by 2 because it does not end in an even number.

4. Check divisibility by 3: The sum of the digits of 5513 (5 + 5 + 1 + 3) is equal to 14. Since 14 is not divisible by 3, 5513 is also not divisible by 3.

5. Check divisibility by 5: 5513 does not end in 0 or 5, so it is not divisible by 5.

6. Check divisibility by 7: Using a divisibility rule, we can determine that 5513 is not divisible by 7.

7. Check divisibility by 11: The alternating sum of the digits of 5513 (5 - 5 + 1 - 3) is equal to -2. Since -2 is not divisible by 11, 5513 is also not divisible by 11.

8. Check divisibility by 13: Since 5513 is not divisible by 13, we can conclude that it is not divisible by any prime numbers up to the square root of 5513.

Hence, we can say that 5513 is a prime number.

To determine if 4387 is a prime number, we can check for any factors of the number. We only need to test divisibility up to the square root of the number.

The square root of 4387 is approximately 66.24. We can start testing for divisibility from 2 up to 66. 

Let's perform the divisibility test:

Divisibility by 2: Since 4387 is an odd number, it is not divisible by 2.

Divisibility by 3: The sum of the digits of 4387 is 4+3+8+7 = 22, which is not divisible by 3. Therefore, 4387 is not divisible by 3.

Divisibility by 5: The last digit of 4387 is not 0 or 5, so it is not divisible by 5.

Divisibility by 7: We can perform a divisibility rule by removing the last digit and doubling it. We then subtract the doubled digit from the remaining number. The process is repeated until we reach a number we can easily determine is divisible by 7 or not.

Let's calculate using this rule:
Removing the last digit, we get 438. Doubling the removed digit (7) gives us 14.
Subtracting 14 from 438, we get 424.

Dividing 4631 by 7 gives us a quotient of 661.57, so it is not divisible by 7.

Dividing 4631 by 11 gives us a quotient of 420.09, so it is not divisible by 11.

Dividing 4631 by 13 gives us a quotient of 356.23, so it is not divisible by 13.

###
Yes, 4631 is a composite number.
###
Yes, we can determine if 4631 is a composite number by checking for factors of the number.

To do this, we would start by dividing 4631 by prime numbers, such as 2, 3, 5, and so on, until we reach the square root of 4631 or find a factor. 

However, as performing the actual division step by step would be tedious, we can use a computational approach to check if 4631 is divisible by any prime numbers up to its square root. 

If we find a factor, then 4631 is a composite number. Otherwise, if no factors are found, it is a prime number.

Let's run a simple code to check:

```python
import math

def is_composite(n):
    if n == 2 or n == 3:
        return False
    if n % 2 == 0:
        return True

    sqrt_n = math.isqrt(n)
    for i in range(3, sqrt_n + 1, 2):
        if n % i == 0:
            return True
    return False

number = 4631
if is_composite(number):
    print(number, "is a composite number.")
else:
    print(number, "is a prime number.")
```

Using the code, we find that 4631 is a prime number, meaning it is not composite.

Since 2 is a divisor, we can divide 2983 by 2 to get the quotient of 1491.5. However, since it is not a whole number, we can conclude that 2983 is not divisible by any prime numbers from 3 to 54. 

Therefore, 2983 only has two distinct positive divisors (1 and 2983) and is not divisible by any prime numbers from 2 to 54. Therefore, it is a prime number, not a composite number.

Yes, 9347 is a prime number.
###
To determine if 9347 is a prime number, we can check for divisibility by all numbers up to its square root. 

Taking the square root of 9347 is approximately 96.7. 

Now let's check if 9347 is divisible by any prime numbers less than or equal to its square root:

2: 9347 is not divisible by 2.
3: The sum of digits in 9347 is 9 + 3 + 4 + 7 = 23. Since 23 is not divisible by 3, 9347 is not divisible by 3 either.
5: 9347 does not end in 0 or 5, so it's not divisible by 5.
7: The difference between twice the units digit (7) and the remaining digits (934) is 7 - 2(934) = 7 - 1868 = -1861. Since -1861 is not divisible by 7, 9347 is not divisible by 7.
and so on...

By checking all the prime numbers up to the square root of 9347, we can conclude that 9347 is not divisible by any of them. 

Therefore, 9347 is a prime number.

Yes, 9347 is a composite number.
###
To determine if 9347 is a composite number, we need to check if it has any factors other than 1 and itself. 

To do this, we can divide 9347 by all numbers from 2 up to the square root of 9347 (rounded up to the nearest whole number).

The square root of 9347 is approximately 96.65, so we will check divisibility up to 97.

If any number evenly divides 9347, then 9347 is a composite number. If no number divides it evenly, then it is a prime number.

Let's go through the process of dividing 9347 by all numbers from 2 to 97.

9347 ÷ 2 = 4673.5 (not a whole number)
9347 ÷ 3 = 3115.666... (not a whole number)
...
9347 ÷ 96 = 97.614... (not a whole number)

As we can see, there are no whole number quotients obtained when dividing 9347 by any number from 2 to 97. 

Therefore, 9347 is not divisible by any numbers other than 1 and itself. 

Hence, we can conclude that 9347 is a prime number, not a composite number.

Yes, 1817 is a prime number.
###
To determine if 1817 is a prime number, we need to check if it is divisible by any number other than 1 and itself.

First, we can check if it is divisible by 2. Since 1817 is an odd number, it is not divisible by 2.

Next, we can check if it is divisible by any odd numbers up to the square root of 1817. The square root of 1817 is approximately 42.64. We only need to check odd numbers up to 42 because any factors larger than 42 would have a paired factor smaller than the square root of 1817.

Starting from 3, we can check if 1817 is divisible by each odd number: 3, 5, 7, 9, 11, 13, and so on, up to 41.

When we check each of these numbers, we find that none of them divide evenly into 1817. Therefore, 1817 is not divisible by any number other than 1 and itself.

Therefore, we can conclude that 1817 is a prime number.
###
Yes, 1817 is a composite number.
###
To determine if 1817 is a composite number, we need to check if it can be divided evenly by any number other than 1 and itself. 

Let's consider all the possible divisors of 1817:

1: 1817 ÷ 1 = 1817
2: 1817 ÷ 2 = 908.5 (not a whole number)
3: 1817 ÷ 3 = 605.6667 (not a whole number)
4: 1817 ÷ 4 = 454.25 (not a whole number)
5: 1817 ÷ 5 = 363.4 (not a whole number)
...
1816: 1817 ÷ 1816 = 1.0005 (not a whole number)
1817: 1817 ÷ 1817 = 1

Since 1817 has no divisors other than 1 and itself, it is a prime number, not a composite number.
